G	G2	PART I : LAND OWNERSHIP, LAND TRANSACTIONS, AND PROPERTY RIGHTS IN THE EXPANSION AREA	1	<p>   <span style="font-size:12px;">The survey has three parts. The first part asks questions about <strong>property ownership and rights</strong> in the expansion areas of the city, the second part focuses on <strong>land use regulations</strong>, and the third part focuses on the <strong>subdivision of land</strong> into residential plots. We are interested in the single answer that applies to <u>all or most</u> of the land in the<em><strong> Expansion Area</strong></em>.
